> **🔒 CUSTODY / NO-LITERALS RULE (supervisor fleet-wide ruling 2026-07-17 — I VIOLATED this; see the incident note below).**
> Real attribution (hive_id / origin / tg_hash / hk) and any vector DERIVED from a real persona are SECRETS and MUST NOT appear as
> literals in ANY tracked artifact — code, comments, examples, test fixtures, docs, RESUME prose, or COMMIT MESSAGES. Documenting a
> secret IS publishing it. **The public-hygiene gate does NOT protect this class** (it matches 12-hex MAC shapes; an 8-hex hive_id /
> tg_hash sails straight through — a green gate is NOT a leak-check). Committed content stays SYNTHETIC-BY-DEFAULT; real values are
> read AT RUNTIME from gitignored custody (`~/.r2-dev-trial/*.bin`, mode 600) or env — the hive-live-view.mjs pattern. "Lock to
> PROVISIONED" ALWAYS means at RUNTIME, never "commit the values". Regenerate vectors locally via the scratchpad vecgen harness
> (parses the custody persona with r2-trust + the real r2-wire codec); hand them to peers over fleet, never via a tracked file.

> **▶ ESP L2CAP CoC FIX — co-review turn (2026-07-16): answered core's one-per-ACL POLICY Q from metal ground truth; NO edit/push/hardware.**
> Core's ARCH-refined design (fixed command slots not stack-local args; fixed NPL pools BLE_HOST_EV_COUNT=19/SEM_COUNT=10
> → one persistent dispatcher event + bounded app ring + app-level FreeRTOS sem/notify pool; logical channel-generation
> handle not chan*; host-owned registry). My caller-contract UNCHANGED (8 sync-Result send_to sites). Core asked ME (metal-usage
> owner) the one-per-ACL policy Q. **ANSWERED (read-only, verified against canonical `crates/r2-esp/src/l2cap.rs` @ r2-core-consolidation):**
> - **CONFIRM one-per-ACL is R2's real model.** Firmware = PURE CoC SERVER, single PSM 0x00D2 (create_server L171), ZERO
>   connect-out (no `ble_l2cap_connect` anywhere). `send_to` (L185-188) resolves by peer_addr → first non-closing channel; a
>   2nd CoC to the same peer_addr is dead weight send_to never selects. R2 has NO USE for >1 CoC/peer. I back enforce-one-per-ACL fail-closed.
> - **Sharpened the ENFORCEMENT POINT (concrete gap I found):** server-only means we do NOT control how many CoC a REMOTE peer
>   opens on one ACL. `handle_accept` (L398-437) has NO per-conn_handle dedup — accepts a 2nd CoC on the same conn_handle
>   unconditionally. Reject there (non-closing PeerChannel already exists for conn_handle → return error rc) → NimBLE refuses
>   the 2nd channel → core's conn_handle-keyed retain (L460/487) becomes correct-by-construction, aliasing killed at source, not peer-trust.
> - `handle_connected` L460 retain already assumes one-per-conn_handle but SILENTLY evicts a live sibling — same aliasing other side; accept-reject fixes both.
> - Completeness: COC_MAX_NUM=3 is the STACK-WIDE ceiling, NOT per-ACL; one-per-ACL → 3 concurrent peers max; more peers = separate config bump (orthogonal).
> - Sent to core (queued, core busy). STILL GATED: co-review the compile-verified rewrite when core routes it (read-only, allowed); metal validation on Roy hardware GO.
>
> **▶ UPDATE (same day): core SUPERSEDED one-per-ACL → GENERATION-PER-CoC-CHANNEL registry** (core-codex's lean; correct for 1 or >1 CoC/ACL;
> DISCONNECTED removes EXACT chan+generation = root fix for sibling-aliasing). My earlier "I back one-per-ACL enforcement at handle_accept" is
> SUPERSEDED — generation-per-chan is a strict superset that drops the need for accept-time dedup. My sync-Result send_to caller-contract + 8 sites
> STILL UNCHANGED (re-confirmed). Core-codex final re-pass tightened INTERNALS (all core-owned, contract untouched): fixed-slot COPIED payload +
> host-ACK-before-free cancellation (no stack-local UAF); UNCONDITIONAL Err on host-task sync-call (fail-closed, not debug_assert); one persistent
> dispatcher event + app-owned completion slots (per-command NPL event/sem would exhaust the fixed pool); nonblocking app-ring enqueue (NPL eventq_put
> blocks portMAX_DELAY). Design CONVERGED per core-codex. Core authors next (pending supervisor scope nod) → routes me the compile-verified rewrite.

> - **CORRECTION (2026-07-16, android refutation WON against source — my earlier "data-path-current@HEAD / relay works" was WRONG on the RAK relay hop):** the multi-hop demo BREAKS as-is at the RAK relay, and it is a CODE DROP not a metal issue. GROUND TRUTH: (a) DFR sensor emits COMPACT on LoRa UNCONDITIONALLY — apiary_bus_task (dfr1195 main.rs:6033-6065) encode_compact, has_route=1, route_stack[0]=(my_hive>>16) upper-16, event_hash=nz.r2.apiary.reading 0x64cedb11, target=my_tg_hash. benchsf7 changes SF ONLY, codec stays compact (NOT SF-gated). (b) RAK handle_rx_frame (r2-dataplane lib.rs:35) = decode_extended(frame) -> Err => return no; r2-dataplane has NO decode_compact + NO transcode (grep empty); RAK RX (rak main.rs:954) feeds raw LoRa bytes straight in. => RAK drops D4's compact frame at decode_extended Err, relay_on NEVER evaluated. The supervisor/core keyless-relay-rule question is MOOT (returns before any relay/keyless logic). This would fire even with a perfect RAK PA — so my earlier "hive-side code-complete, only metal PA-radiate unknown" was INCOMPLETE: the push_masked->transmit wiring IS complete, but handle_rx_frame never reaches it for a compact frame. XIAO SEAM: xiao_bridge_task (main.rs:5141) decode_compact + forwards COMPACT verbatim to phone (USB SYNC flags bit0=0x00=compact-stream, [len u16 LE][frame]); NO transcode to extended, NO origin zero-extend. So the intended demo path is COMPACT end-to-end EXCEPT the RAK relay. FIX is CORE-owned (r2-dataplane): add compact-tier RX/relay to handle_rx_frame (keep the wire compact through the relay — transcode-at-RAK would break the compact-only XIAO+phone). > - **WIRE CONTRACT PUBLISHED (nz.r2.apiary.reading COMPACT origin, 29B, byte-exact from apiary_bus_task + r2-wire compact.rs/hmac.rs):** [0]=0x06 (ver0|Event|R|H) [1]=0x53 (ttl5|k3) [2..4]=msg_id u16 BE (apiary seq, from 1) [4..8]=event_hash BE=0x64cedb11 (BUTTON=nz.r2.apiary.button distinct) [8..12]=target BE=my_tg_hash (provisioned <PROV-TG-HASH>; code literal <DEMO-TG-HASH> STALE) [12]=route_len 1 [13..15]=route_stack[0] u16 BE=(my_hive>>16) upper-16 (provisioned D4 <D4-HIVE-ID>-><D4-ORIGIN>; code literal <FALLBACK-ORIGIN> STALE=unprovisioned mac_low3) [15..21]=payload 6B RAW seq(u32 BE)+value(i16 BE, sinf*1000 +/-1000) NOT CBOR (payload seq independent of header msg_id) [21..29]=HMAC-8 = HMAC-SHA256(persona hk) over authenticated_bytes_compact = msg_type|msg_id(2BE)|origin(2BE=route[0])|event_hash(4BE)|target(4BE)|payload(6)=19B, flags EXCLUDED. Origin = compact 16-bit upper-half of FNV-32; full 32-bit NOT on compact wire (resolve <D4-ORIGIN>->D4). Multi-hop = route_stack(16-bit entries)+TTL5; relay appends 16-bit (§9.2, once core adds compact relay); XIAO=transparent verbatim compact forward (no append, USB SYNC flag compact 0x00). Published to supervisor for android+composer; flagged for specs canon. Origin frame STABLE regardless of core's relay-side fix.

> - **★ FORWARD-SECRECY GAP in the join seal — composer raised it, I VERIFIED + SHARPENED it (spec-level, NOT custody hygiene). FORWARD SECRECY WOULD CLOSE THE MEASUREMENT PATH WE NOW DEPEND ON.** A real tradeoff, not a free fix — anyone proposing FS must answer "then how does the issuer attest what it sealed?" >   - **CRACK 1 — core's premise "DATA_TX_LORA is the ONLY way onto the LoRa carrier" is FALSE.** The real carrier edge is `lora.send`, and it has **TWO** sites: main.rs:5043 (the DATA_TX_LORA drain core enumerated) **and main.rs:5055 — `build_lora_beacon` → `lora.send`, bypassing DATA_TX_LORA entirely**, inside `lora_route_task` (cfg `loraroute`) ⇒ **it IS in the demo image.** Core enumerated a QUEUE that FEEDS the edge. **Core's conclusion survives via an argument core never made:** the missed sender emits a §8.1 discovery beacon (magic 0xB2, ver 0x01, ≤17B) built by DIRECT byte-assembly at main.rs:4684 — it never touches `encode_extended`, so it cannot carry an extended frame.
>   - **CRACK 2 — core's "xiao_bridge_task:5419 is compact BY CONSTRUCTION, phone-originated" is FALSE.** It is an **UNVALIDATED OPAQUE PASSTHROUGH**: `copy_from_slice(&inbuf[3..3+bl])` → `try_send`, **no decode, no format check**. The 2 `decode_compact` calls in that task are the OPPOSITE direction (LoRa→USB egress; its own comment: *"the phone does the authoritative verify_compact"*). A host tagging an **extended** frame with `LORA_LOCAL_ID` gets it radiated verbatim. Compact by **HOST CONVENTION**, not construction.
>   - **SCOPE, HONESTLY — crack 2 does NOT touch the demo, twice over:** (i) 5419 is `cfg(feature="xiaobridge")`; the demo compose is `fakesensor,benchsf7,dev,baked_persona` and `fakesensor = [otaengine, loraroute, loratcxo]` ⇒ xiaobridge NOT pulled ⇒ **task compiled OUT**; (ii) independently, 5419 is the **phone→LoRa** direction while the demo data path is sensor→LoRa→bridge→phone — **the opposite way**. Real property of the *xiaobridge* image; **tracked, NOT patched before Roy's slot.**
>   - **★ THE PROOF THAT ACTUALLY HOLDS (demo image, by construction):** `lora.send` = exactly 2 sites, both in `lora_route_task`. **5043** ← DATA_TX_LORA ← senders: `mesh_broadcast:4199` (sole caller **6143**, traced to `encode_compact`) + `xiao_bridge_task:5419` (compiled out under fakesensor). **5055** ← `build_lora_beacon` (direct assembly, never `encode_extended`). ⇒ **every byte reaching the LoRa carrier in the demo image is either `encode_compact` or a §8.1 beacon. No extended, by construction — closed over the REAL edge.** ⇒ **VERDICT UNCHANGED: GO TO METAL.**
>   - **★★ THE RULE (banked in [[never-conclude-from-a-null]]): CLOSE OVER THE ACTUAL BOUNDARY, NOT A PROXY FOR IT.** *"Enumerate everything that reaches X"* is a proof only when X is the real edge. Ask **"what is the LAST thing before the air/disk/socket?"** and enumerate THAT — a queue/channel/wrapper is an *implementation* of the edge and there can be a second one. **Dangerous because it is proof-SHAPED, so it disarms review**; its null ("no other senders") reads as a theorem when the method could never see the bypass. **Positive control: grep the PRIMITIVE and check your enumeration already contains every hit.** You pick the proxy because it's where the DESIGN says data flows — **but the bypass never read the design.**
>   - **HONEST SYMMETRY:** core was right that my count couldn't prove there was no 7th site — there were in fact **EIGHT** `encode_extended` sites, not 6 (**1783** + **5949**), and **both go to `socket.send_to` (UDP/WiFi), where extended is canon-legal**. So my count was wrong **AND harmless**, exactly as core's method predicts. **Core's METHOD beat mine; my EXECUTION beat core's. Keep both halves.**

>   - **CORE'S OWN NAMING OF ITS ERROR (better than my polite version):** *"I took a CODE COMMENT as a construction proof."* :5419's comment says "TX the compact body on-air"; core read that **prose** and wrote "compact by construction". *"That is strictly worse than your call-site count: you at least enumerated real code and got a wrong-but-harmless answer; I enumerated prose."*
>   - **★★ THE RULE, IN ITS FINAL FORM (core's sharpening of my diagnosis — keep this one):** *"You picked the queue because the queue is where the DESIGN says frames go — but the beacon never read the design."* ⇒ **a proxy-closure only covers the paths that OBEY the architecture, so it is exactly blind to the bypass — and a bypass is the only thing a closure proof exists to catch. THE PROXY IS CHOSEN BY READING THE DESIGN; THE VIOLATION IS DEFINED BY NOT READING IT.** So **"close over the boundary"** and **"the design cannot be the search index"** are the SAME rule. **Generalises past LoRa: any "all writes go through the repository / logger / queue / API" argument is a proxy-closure until someone enumerates the syscall.** Sits beside the day's other two — *state the SCOPE with the result* (a null needs a positive control) and *close over the EDGE* (a closure needs the real boundary): **both are one disease — a confident green over the wrong universe.**
>   - **★ MY REFUTATION OF CORE'S MITIGATION — the finding is SHARPER than core's own sharpening.** Core softened it: *"the host is paired (r2-usb-pair), so this is not a stranger-on-the-wire — but trusted host is an authorisation argument, not a conformance one."* Right about the KIND of argument; **WRONG on the fact. PAIRING DOES NOT GATE THE LoRa TX PRIMITIVE** (VERIFIED main.rs:5410-5419): the demux has **three SIBLING branches** — `looks_control(0xFF)` → `pairing.handle` → `persist_link_key`; `!synced && looks_sync` → consume SYNC; **`plen>1 && inbuf[2]==LORA_LOCAL_ID` → `copy_from_slice` → `DATA_TX_LORA.try_send`**. The third checks **NO** pairing state, **NO** link_key, and does **NOT** require `synced` — **it SETS `synced=true`**. `persisted_link_key` is loaded (:5220) and handed to `Peripheral::new` (:5228), then **NEVER consulted on the TX path** (grep positive-controlled: 11 `pairing` hits ⇒ the null is real; link_key touches = :299/:304 load, :2726/:2742 flash record, :5399/:5406-7 inside the pairing branch — **none gate the radiate**). ⇒ **an UNPAIRED host, with NO SYNC, that never ran the SM, can radiate.** The pairing SM runs **ALONGSIDE** the primitive, not **IN FRONT OF** it ⇒ **it provides ZERO protection here.** The only real bound is **PHYSICAL USB ACCESS** — the same bound with or without pairing. **So: not "a paired host can radiate any bytes" — "ANY host that can reach the port can radiate any bytes."** Both of core's axes survive; the authorisation axis no longer softens it.
>   - **★★ NEW COROLLARY (banked in [[never-conclude-from-a-null]]): WE AUDIT *ESCALATIONS* HARDER THAN *DE-ESCALATIONS*, SO DE-ESCALATIONS ARE WHERE UNVERIFIED CLAIMS SURVIVE.** Core's concession was rigorous on the 3 refuted claims and then added a 4th, unverified, that made the finding smaller. **Not motivated — the same reflex as "compact by construction": a plausible fact read off the DESIGN instead of the code.** The SM *is* there, *is* wired, *looks* like it guards the port. **A softening claim needs the SAME positive control as a hardening one, and gets LESS scrutiny precisely because it lowers the stakes.** ⇒ **Applies to MY OWN de-escalations** ("only cosmetic", "compiled out", "not on the demo path") — each is a claim; scope-verify it as hard as an alarm.
>   - **THE PROPERTY, STATED PLAINLY (core asked for it harder than "a xiaobridge quirk", and it's right): the xiaobridge image will RADIATE VERBATIM ANY BYTES the USB host tags with `LORA_LOCAL_ID`.** Not "may carry extended" — **ANY bytes.** An **arbitrary-LoRa-transmit primitive exposed to the host**, whose conformance consequence is that the image can violate **R2-LORA §5.1** at the host's discretion **with no code in the DFR disagreeing.** **Tracked: hive task #69. NOT patched before Roy's slot** (flashed image in the proven anchor path ⇒ unpriced risk, zero demo benefit).
>   - **⚠ SPEC Q ROUTED TO SPECS — I HAVE THE PATCH READY AND DELIBERATELY WILL NOT PICK THE RULING THAT SUITS IT:** is an MCU bridge **REQUIRED** to enforce bearer tier on host-originated frames (⇒ DFR non-conformant TODAY, validate MANDATORY), **or** is the **R2-USB seam a TRUST BOUNDARY** where §5.1 conformance is the **HOST's** obligation (⇒ fix belongs in R2-USB as a host MUST; my validate is defence-in-depth)? **Beyond my patch:** if the seam is trusted, **EVERY** bridge implementing §3.5 is an arbitrary-transmit primitive for its host **BY DESIGN** and the spec should say so; if not, §3.5 needs an explicit *"the bridge MUST reject frames violating the target bearer tier"* and every existing bridge is non-conformant until it validates. **§5.1 names the tier rule but names no ENFORCEMENT POINT at a host seam — so nobody enforced it.** (Mirror of the day's other canon item: *a physical limit is not a conformance check*.) Candidate fix post-ruling: byte0/`decode_compact` validate before `try_send`, reject non-compact, real error to the phone instead of silent garbage on the air.

>   - **SPECS' READ ON THE FIX (advisory): (1) — the validate is a CONFORMANCE fix, not defence-in-depth — but NOT because the host is untrusted. Because "§5.1 binds the BEARER, and you ARE the bearer."** The `faculty` framing seals it: **a faculty is the only part of the organism touching the air, so it is the only place the bearer invariant CAN be enforced — not because it distrusts the rest of itself.** ⇒ **MY PATCH MUST BE A TIER CHECK, NEVER A PAIRING/AUTH GATE**: a pairing gate fixes nothing (a paired host can still send extended) **AND** would contradict `R2-USB:32/:260/:329`. Also: specs named my question a **FALSE DICHOTOMY** — trust and conformance are **independent axes**; option (2)'s premise ("the seam is a trust boundary") is **foreclosed**, but that does *not* make §5.1 the host's obligation. *"My TCP stack trusts my own application completely and still won't emit a malformed IP packet."*
>   - **★★ MY CHALLENGE 1 — "THE DFR IS NON-CONFORMANT TODAY" OVERSTATES IT, and the distinction IS the spec gap.** §5.1's MUST NOT binds **BEHAVIOUR**. The DFR only violates it if it **EMITS** extended — and today the host sends compact, so **it does not**. Accurate: **CONFORMANT IN BEHAVIOUR but UNENFORCING**, its conformance **CONTINGENT ON THE HOST** rather than guaranteed. ⇒ **THE REAL QUESTION: does a MUST NOT bind only BEHAVIOUR, or also require an ENFORCEMENT POINT at the last node that can still stop it?** Canon does not say — **that ambiguity IS the gap**. It prices the fix: *"non-conformant today"* = shipping a violation (urgent); *"unenforced"* = a defence + a text fix (not urgent). **Specs is right about the FIX and wrong about the LABEL.**
>   - **★★ MY CHALLENGE 2 — §5.1 IS INTERNALLY INCONSISTENT (sharper than either of us framed).** Sentence 1: *"The extended format… **MUST NOT** be used on the LoRa bearer"* — **ABSOLUTE**. Closing sentence: *"If 32-byte-HMAC extended-e2e is ever required on LoRa it needs a **Roy-gated NAMED PHY profile** whose MTU ≥ the signed-extended size (e.g. `SF9/BW125` = 115 B, or a BW250 profile)"* — **CONDITIONAL**. **It cannot be both.** It **reads as absolute and means profile-conditional**; the live thread must pick one.
>   - **★★★ AND THE ACCIDENT HAS ALREADY STOPPED HIDING IT — NOT IN A FUTURE PROFILE, ON ROY'S BENCH TONIGHT.** Specs located the escape at SF9/115 B as *prospective*. **It is not prospective.** §5.1's ENTIRE stated rationale is the 54 B signed-extended floor vs the **51 B SF12/BW125** MTU. But **`R2-LORA:401`: `lora_mtu` BW125 = SF7-8 → **222 B**, SF9 → 115 B, SF10-12 → 51 B**, and **the demo runs `benchsf7`** — a profile **canon itself blesses** (`:386` *"a labelled WHOLE-MESH SF7/BW125 profile"*). ⇒ **On the profile Roy powers up tonight, extended fits with 168 B to spare, §5.1's justification is ALREADY DEAD, and the MUST NOT survives ON TEXT ALONE.** **`ef6f95a` is the ONLY thing enforcing §5.1 on that board, and it is 6 hours old. The rule has been unenforced on SF7 for as long as SF7 has existed.** ⇒ core's *gate-it* call was right for a **stronger reason than either of us gave**: it is not tidying a wart. Banked as memory [[s5-1-extended-on-lora-rests-on-text-alone]].

>   - **★★ SPECS CHALLENGED MY STRONGEST CLAIM ("the justification is ALREADY DEAD") — RIGHT INSTINCT, REFUTED BY THEIR OWN TABLE.** Their steelman: maybe §5.1 rests on **ToA**, not MTU (`:401` *"1/s at 10% needs ToA ≤ 100 ms → only SF7 qualifies (all sizes ≤ 51 B)"*), so 54 B busts the envelope ⇒ my claim is only *half* dead. **REFUTED, structurally: ToA is a function of SIZE, not FORMAT** — a 54 B compact and a 54 B extended frame have **identical** airtime ⇒ ToA **cannot ground a format-keyed MUST NOT**. The floor-steelman (extended ≥54 B always) dies on canon's **own rows**: `:377` *"These rows are COMPACT-format sizes"*, **SF7 = 51 B→103 ms, 115 B→195 ms, 222 B→348 ms**; a 54 B extended frame at SF7 ≈ **110 ms**. ⇒ **canon TABULATES compact frames at SF7 costing 195 ms and 348 ms as legitimate operating points — 2× and 3× the airtime of the extended frame it FORBIDS.** A ToA rationale would ban 54 B extended while blessing 222 B compact at 3× the cost. **No coherent rule does that.** ⇒ **§5.1 states EXACTLY ONE ground (MTU); the paragraph never mentions airtime. MY CLAIM STANDS UNQUALIFIED: on SF7 the justification is not half dead — it is dead.** *What survives of their instinct:* extended costs **+24 B for the same content** (32 B vs 8 B HMAC) — the apiary 29 B/67 ms reading → ~53 B/~105 ms, ~1.6× airtime, marginally busting 1/s@10%. **A real efficiency reason to prefer compact; NOT the ground of a MUST NOT.** *Free nit:* `:401`'s takeaway overstates its own table — **SF7/51 B = 103 ms = 0.97/s**, already missing both 1/s and 100 ms. ⇒ asked specs to **DROP/RECAST their proposed 3rd defect**; the real one is *"canon states a rationale that DOES NOT BIND on the bench profile canon itself blesses (`:386` labelled WHOLE-MESH SF7/BW125)"*.
>   - **★★ NEW GROUND TRUTH I DID NOT HAVE — verified both: `R2-USB:98` *"USB uses COMPACT R2-WIRE format… This matches BLE and LoRa"*; `R2-USB:100` *"An implementation MAY negotiate EXTENDED format via the SYNC handshake (§3.3) if both ends support it."*** ⇒ **MY BRIDGE IGNORES THAT NEGOTIATION ENTIRELY** — the SYNC branch comment is literally *"version/flags negotiation ignored for the MVP"*. So it **never assents to extended** ⇒ satisfies specs' first horn (*"either never negotiates extended"*) — **BY ACCIDENT, NOT BY CONSTRUCTION.** **Ignoring a negotiation ≠ refusing one:** a host that sends extended **without** negotiating still gets it radiated. ⇒ **specs' two horns are NOT EXHAUSTIVE for a real implementation — there is a THIRD state, NEGOTIATION-IGNORING: conformant on the handshake, unenforcing on the air.** Flagged for §3.3.

>   - **★ MY REFINEMENT TO THE RULING (offered; specs may decline):** their formulation **over-reaches** — taken literally, *"WOULD radiate if fed"* makes conformance mean **PROVABLY-CANNOT-VIOLATE**, which no real system meets (**my io_task "would" emit extended too, if someone flipped a cfg**) ⇒ the word does no work in the *other* direction. **THE LINE I THINK THEY WANT: CONFORMANCE IS A PROPERTY OVER THE *DESIGNED INPUT DOMAIN*** — conformant iff the invariant holds for **all inputs the device is DESIGNED TO ACCEPT**. Bridge domain = *"any framed bytes the host sends"* (**that IS its function**, per `R2-USB:32` — the host is not a foreign party but the same organism) ⇒ extended is **inside** it ⇒ **non-conformant, no malice or mistake required**. io_task's domain **excludes** *"an extended frame to radiate"* — reaching it requires **EDITING THE BUILD, not supplying an input** ⇒ **conformant**. Keeps the teeth, drops the over-reach, **and is TESTABLE**. ⇒ **It is the egress-closure rule pointed at the ingress: for ENFORCEMENT close over the EGRESS (cannot be outflanked); for CONFORMANCE close over the INPUT DOMAIN.**

> - **✅✅ CORE'S §5.1 ESCAPE-HATCH UNSOUNDNESS — VERIFIED, AND §5.1'S *OWN CITED AUTHORITY* CONVICTS IT.** Core's argument: MTU was never the real obstacle — compact/extended aren't self-describing, so a receiver **MIS-PARSES** the wrong tier rather than rejecting it; **raising the MTU creates NO discriminator**, so the hatch licenses exactly the failure the rule exists to prevent. **CONFIRMED FROM SOURCE, and the spec convicts itself:** §5.1:326 cites *"R2-WIRE §4.3.5 **format-detection**"* as though a discriminator existed. **`R2-WIRE.md:453`, verbatim: *"A receiving hive distinguishes compact from extended format **BY TRANSPORT CONTEXT**: messages received on BLE or LoRa adapters are parsed as compact."*** ⇒ **IT DETECTS NOTHING — IT ASSUMES.** The section named *Format Detection* hard-codes format per bearer, so **a LoRa receiver parses everything as compact BY SPEC** ⇒ an extended frame on LoRa isn't rejected, it's **mis-parsed**. Core was right and didn't need me to be.
>   - **★★ MY STRENGTHENING — THE HATCH IS NOT A PHY DECISION, IT IS A BREAKING WIRE CHANGE.** If Roy gated the SF9/115 B profile, **§4.3.5:453 would STILL mandate "messages received on LoRa adapters are parsed as compact"** ⇒ **every conformant receiver on that profile mis-parses the very extended frames the profile exists to carry.** So the hatch needs a **THREE-way change**: an in-band **discriminator (a wire change)** + amend **§4.3.5** + amend **§5.1**. **It READS like "Roy approves a PHY profile" and MEANS "break the wire format."** ⇒ **THE HATCH UNDERSTATES ITS OWN COST BY AN ORDER OF MAGNITUDE** — a stronger reason to kill it than inconsistency: it's **mispriced in a way that invites someone to grant it cheaply.**
>   - **★ NEW — THE DEAD MTU RATIONALE IS *DUPLICATED*, so fixing §5.1 alone leaves the corpse in R2-WIRE.** `§4.3.5:463`: *"On LoRa this is moot: the LoRa bearer is compact-only (R2-LORA §5.1), and a signed extended frame cannot even fit the SF12/BW125 MTU (54-byte floor > 51, R2-LORA §5.2)."* **Same MTU argument, same SF12 scoping, same death on SF7.**

Two specs, one pattern.** Core has routed the re-grounding to specs: **base the MUST NOT on SINGLE-TIER-PER-BEARER** (no in-band discriminator ⇒ mixed tiers structurally undecodable ⇒ **binds on EVERY profile**), demote MTU to a **coincidental SF12-only enforcer**, and **KILL the hatch** (extended-on-LoRa would need a **discriminator = a wire change, not airtime**).

So the member compose is dead **IFF the RAK hears only D4** — non-deterministic if a 2nd transmitter is intermittent (**two runs of the same demo can differ** — worse than deterministic failure). **PIN THE TOPOLOGY, not just the compose.**

> - **★★★ THE TIER DISCRIMINATOR IS *SPENT*, NOT *ABSENT* — and it REFUTES core's proposed §5.1 re-grounding before it reaches canon. VERIFIED AT SOURCE, banked as [[tier-discriminator-is-spent-not-absent]].**
>   - **CORE'S CLAIMS — ALL VERIFIED EXACTLY (not banked):** `R2-LORA.md:349` **verbatim** — *"**Beacon-vs-data demux on the shared LoRa carrier (MUST).** A receiver distinguishes an R2-BEACON §8.1.1 LoRa beacon from a data frame by **content + length**, NOT a carrier prefix: a beacon is the {15,16,17}-byte form with `magic = 0xB2` at offset 0."* · `types.rs:124` `return Err(WireError::InvalidVersion)` with `decode_byte0` requiring `ver == 0` · `0xB2 >> 6 = 2` ⇒ **a beacon CANNOT mint a `CompactFrame`** ⇒ **core's own `Frame = CompactFrame` would have made discovery UNSENDABLE — they caught it themselves, the first self-catch of the day.** · `r2-transport/src/transport.rs:248` `fn send(&self, target: u32, frame: &[u8]) -> Result<(), SendError>` — **untyped bytes, generic, 5+ impls ⇒ core-owned.**
>   - **★★ THEIR SPEC ARGUMENT UNDERSTATES ITSELF.** Core: *"canon knows how to do in-band demux, it just NEVER GAVE compact/extended one."* **VERIFIED SHARPER — canon GAVE them one and SPENT IT ON THE SAME VALUE TWICE:** `compact.rs:54` and `extended.rs:50` are **THE SAME CALL** — `buf[0] = encode_byte0(h.version, h.msg_type, h.flags)`. `decode_byte0` rejects `ver != 0` ⇒ **3 of 4 version values (1,2,3) UNUSED.** And **the beacon demux works PRECISELY BECAUSE the beacon uses ver=2** — it is discriminable **by the very field the two tiers left identical.** ⇒ **THE DISCRIMINATOR IS PRESENT, 2 BITS WIDE, 3 OF 4 VALUES FREE, AND BOTH TIERS WERE ASSIGNED ver=0.** `§4.3.5:453`'s *"detection by transport context"* is a workaround for a **SOLVED** problem left unsolved in one place.
>   - **★★★ ⇒ THIS REFUTES CORE'S RE-GROUNDING AS WORDED.** *"No in-band discriminator ⇒ mixed tiers are **STRUCTURALLY** undecodable — binds on EVERY profile"* is **FALSE.** They are undecodable **BY CHOICE**, one spent value away from decodable. **Same over-claim shape as core's other four** (prose-as-proof → proxy-as-boundary → architecture-as-mitigation → proxy-as-boundary-in-a-type → **structural-from-current-state**) — *"count is now five, one shape"* — **and this one would have gone into CANON.** ⇒ **A rule needs a ground that is TRUE, not merely CURRENTLY TRUE**: a re-grounding on "structurally impossible" gets refuted **the day someone reads `types.rs`**, and then the MUST NOT has lost its **SECOND** ground in a week (the MTU one is already dead on benchsf7).
>   - **THE HONEST GROUND (still core's): mixed tiers are undecodable BECAUSE BOTH FORMATS WERE ASSIGNED ver=0** — contingent, fixable, **and the fix converts a MIS-PARSE into a clean `Err`**, which is the property core actually cares about: **today** an extended frame on LoRa **passes** `decode_byte0` (ver=0 ✓) then garbages; **at ver=1, TODAY'S UNMODIFIED DECODER returns `InvalidVersion` — it FAILS CLOSED.** ⚠ **I did NOT prescribe ver=1** — core's crate, and the cost is real: `version` is a **protocol version**, so tier-tagging it spends version space (2 bits = 4 values) and makes tier×version a product; a free **flag bit** may be better (`b & 0x07`) — **unverified, and not mine to design.** **My only claim: "structurally undecodable" is NOT AVAILABLE AS A PREMISE.**
>   - **★ AND IT RE-AIMS THE HATCH KILL (strengthening it):** with a discriminator the SF9 hatch becomes **SOUND** — a named profile *could* carry extended if receivers could tell. ⇒ **kill it not as "unsound forever" but as "unsound AS WRITTEN: it grants a PHY PROFILE where a WIRE DISCRIMINATOR is required, and prices that wire change at ZERO."** **My mispricing argument survives intact; core's unsoundness argument becomes CONDITIONAL on the byte0 assignment.**
>   - **CORE'S SELF-REFUTATION IS RIGHT AND THE SUM TYPE IS THE ANSWER: `LoRaTransport::Frame = LoRaFrame { Data(CompactFrame), Beacon(BeaconFrame) }`** — it closes **all three senders at the REAL edge** (which the queue newtype structurally cannot) and **encodes `:349`'s beacon-demux MUST in the type.** **Safe precisely because `:349` HAS a real discriminator — the type REFLECTS an invariant canon states correctly. The tier arm does NOT have that. Do the sum; don't let it pretend the tier arm is as well-grounded as the beacon arm.** Trait change is **ruling-independent**; only the per-bearer `Frame` **bindings** await specs (WiFi/IP's binding is exactly where `§4.3.5:463`'s verbatim-forward exception lands). **Core-sequenced: specs re-grounding → design + heads-up to me and composer → land. > - **★★ CORE'S GENERALISATION — the most valuable output of the day, and bigger than LoRa: "A PHYSICAL LIMIT IS NOT A CONFORMANCE CHECK — it only HIDES the violation on the profile where the limit binds."** Review question for specs: **WHICH OF OUR MUSTs ARE ONLY "ENFORCED" BY A LIMIT SOME FUTURE PROFILE REMOVES?** Wherever a spec MUST coincides with a physical constraint, **the MUST is UNTESTED** — and the day someone widens the constraint (a bench profile, a faster PHY, a bigger MTU) the violation ships silently. **MY COROLLARY:** the constraint is often removed by the SAFEST-LOOKING change — `benchsf7` exists purely to make the demo fast, and it is what unmasked a 7-day-old canon violation. **A convenience knob removed an accidental safety property nobody knew they were relying on.** Routed to specs.

> - **★ WHY IT'S LIVE ON THE BENCH BUT INVISIBLE IN THE FIELD (core's catch, and it's sharp):** a SIGNED extended frame is 22B hdr + 32B HMAC = **54B floor > the 51B SF12/BW125 control-profile MTU**, and §5.2 rejects over-MTU **with no fragmentation** => on the FIELD SF12 profile a signed extended frame is **physically un-transmittable** and the bug can never show. **The demo runs benchsf7 (SF7/BW125 = 222B MTU) — which is EXACTLY what makes the non-conformant leg emittable. The bench profile is the unmasker.** My io_task LoRa emissions are a MIX: **4 signed** (sign_extended -> encode_extended -> mesh_broadcast) + **2 forward/relay re-encodes**. HAZARD (why it's worse than a dropped frame): a Compact-mode RAK does NOT cleanly Err on extended — extended byte0 is structurally decodable (same ver|type|flags packing) => decode_compact MIS-PARSES it, and with core's #2 (any heard frame forms a LINK) it would form a neighbour under a **GARBAGE hive_id**, then relay-opaque re-broadcast garbage (TTL/dedup-bounded, but pollutes the table + burns airtime). There is NO reliable in-band discriminator — which is precisely WHY canon makes the bearer single-tier.

> - **⚠ PHRASING HAZARD (android nearly mis-asserted off my wording — propagated fleet-wide):** the route/origin wire field is a **u16 whose VALUE is (hive_id >> 16)**. > **▶ RE-PASS ROUND 2 (2026-07-16) — hive-codex read-only re-pass of the amended commit returned 3 findings; all triaged, NO PUSH.**
> - **F1 (HIGH, CI blocker) — first fix was itself fail-OPEN; SUPERSEDED by round 4 (see below).** The
>   `m=$(grep … | … | sort)` substitutions abort the docs step under Actions' `bash -e -o pipefail` when a
>   grep matches NOTHING (clean) or all matches are allowlisted. My round-2 fix wrapped the WHOLE pipeline in
>   `|| true` — which ALSO swallowed a scanner CRASH (rc>1: bad pattern, missing grep) and mapped it to a clean
>   result. hive-codex round-4 caught that as a NEW fail-open. Correct fix is in round 4: a `scan()` helper that
>   treats grep rc 0/1 as success but PROPAGATES rc>1 (fail-closed), with `|| true` on ONLY the allowlist filter.
> - **F3 (MED, test weakness) — DONE.** `kat()` now accepts optional `reason` ([MAC]/[TAIL]/[TAIL-0x]/[TAIL-COMPACT]) and exact `count`; high-value KATs assert them so a wrong-CLASSIFIER regression (MAC misread as TAIL, or the 4-group run's 2-window count) can no longer stay green on a bare flag/no-flag check. Selftest **41/41** with the stricter asserts.
> - **F2 (MED, false-positives) — VERIFIED, one sub-claim REFUTED, narrowing DEFERRED as a Roy-canon tradeoff.**
>   (Examples described abstractly here on purpose — writing the literal token beside a context word would trip
>   this very gate on RESUME.md; see the self-inflicted-trap note in memory.) Confirmed latent FPs, all currently
>   ABSENT from the tree: a time-of-day triple or a short two-digit-group date sitting beside a board/device word
>   classifies as a TAIL; a six-digit baud constant beside a board-id label classifies as a compact tail; a
>   revision-like six-hex filename segment can too. REFUTED: ISO-date *filenames* with a four-digit year do NOT
>   flag — the hex negative-lookbehind already blocks them (the year's last digit is hex before the date run).
>   Decision: the gate is fail-SAFE by design (errs toward flagging, exact-allowlist escape hatch); every F2 fix
>   narrows CONTEXT = the fail-OPEN direction that burned this workstream twice, and the real tree is currently
>   clean (exit 0). Not narrowing unilaterally; routed to hive-codex/supervisor as a noise-vs-fail-open tradeoff on
>   Roy-canon context rules. **Do-not-assume:** narrowing the tail-context set to quiet F2 without KATs proving no
>   new fail-open is the exact regression class this branch exists to kill.

>   separator characters (`next if token has both ':' and '-'`), so a 6-pair MAC written with mixed separators

>   extraction case. Selftest **43/43**; full gate over the real tree still clean (exit 0) → flagging mixed adds

> **▶ RE-PASS ROUND 4 (2026-07-16) — hive-codex refuted my OWN round-2/3 fixes; both were real. FIXED. NO PUSH.**
> - **docs F1 fail-OPEN (HIGH) — properly FIXED.** The round-2 blanket `|| true` mapped a scanner CRASH (grep
>   rc>1: missing binary, invalid pattern, unreadable tree) to the same empty/clean result as a legit no-match —
>   fail-open. Replaced with a `scan()` helper: grep rc 0/1 = success (emit matches, empty on no-match), rc>1
>   PROPAGATES so `set -e` aborts = fail-CLOSED; `|| true` now wraps ONLY the allowlist filter (its rc1 = all
>   placeholders, never a tool failure). Verified end-to-end incl. the decisive case: a broken grep (rc2) now
>   makes the step EXIT 2 (fail-closed), not exit-0-clean. Clean→0, planted MAC→1, allowlisted-only→0 all hold.
> - **kat() crash-suppression (MED) — FIXED.** `kat()` used `hygiene_scan || true`, so a scanner crash on a
>   VALID must-pass fixture false-passed. Now captures the scanner status (`&& src=0 || src=$?`) and FAILs the
>   KAT on any non-zero on valid input; the malformed-stream crash path is checked separately. Proved with an
>   injected `hygiene_scan(){ return 3; }` — kat() reports FAIL (old code printed ok). Selftest **43/43**.
> - **merge-legitimate-fragments precision (noise, NOT fail-open) — documented tradeoff.** A timestamp+segment
>   like a time triple joined by a separator to another triple normalises to six pairs and flags [MAC]; spaced
>   fragments pass. Inherently ambiguous; under the fail-SAFE policy this is a noise tradeoff, not a hole. Policy:
>   keep flagging (fail-safe); if a real doc trips it, use a `T`/space separator or an exact allowlist entry.
>
> **▶ RE-PASS ROUND 5 (2026-07-16) — hive-codex found my round-4 fix STILL had two fail-opens. FIXED. NO PUSH.**
> - **docs allowlist filter fail-OPEN (HIGH) — FIXED.** Round 4 fixed the primary `scan()` grep but left the
>   allowlist step as `{ grep -vixE … || true; }`. That `|| true` ALSO swallowed a filter tool failure (rc>1): if
>   the allowlist grep errored while upstream emitted a REAL MAC, the leak was erased and the pipeline read clean.
>   Reproduced. Fixed with an `allow_filter` helper (same rc discipline as `scan`): rc0/1 = success, rc>1 propagates
>   = fail-CLOSED. Verified: allowlist-grep rc2 + upstream real MAC now EXITS NONZERO, not clean.
> - **end-to-end KATs discarded exit status (MED) — FIXED.** The `hygiene_scan_tree` KATs used `[ -n "$(…)" ]` /
>   `[ -z … ]`, which drop the command-substitution status, so a scanner crash that emitted a finding (or emitted
>   nothing) false-passed. Replaced with an `e2e MODE NAME` helper that captures output AND status separately:
>   flag = findings+rc0, clean = empty+rc0, failclosed = rc≠0. The empty-tree KAT is the one explicit rc≠0 case.
> - RESUME durable line corrected (no longer claims blanket `|| true`); strongest temp-repo mixed-EUI/mixed-separator
>   replay recorded PASS (both mixed orders + mixed EUI-64 + underscore/-if00 path form all flag [MAC] end-to-end;
>   allowlisted placeholder passes). F4/Pages branch stays HELD (supervisor-codex: publication policy, not a hygiene

## 🔬 XIAO BENCH decode-support (android, 2026-07-12) — golden frames handed + board-health cleared (commit 95d5148)
android hit two things decoding the XIAO USB egress: (1) InvalidRouteLen on live captures, (2) the stream went QUIET.
**Both answered via fleet send + persisted to docs/BENCH-BOARD-FACTS.md.** (1) ROOT CAUSE = capture drop, NOT a
decoder bug: `dd bs=1` byte-drops the egress (27–30B vs true fixed 31B); byte0=0x06 sets has_route, so ONE dropped
byte reads data[12] as rlen=0x00 = InvalidRouteLen exactly. Handed a byte-exact GOLDEN frame from canonical
`r2_wire::encode_compact` (round-trips decode_compact): compact 31B = `0653000164cedbf305fe0701011234a10018eaa101182a0102030405060708`;
R2-USB DATA record 33B = `1f00…` (1f00 = payload_len 31 LE). Emitter LANDED = `crates/r2-hive-bin/examples/gen_golden_compact_frame.rs`
(regen: `cargo run -p r2-hive --example gen_golden_compact_frame`). 0xA1 sighting golden already byte-exact in
dfr1195 `USB-BEACON-SIGHTING-FORMAT.md` KAT. (2) QUIET = peer-silence (egress is PURE forwarded LoRa RX, NO
keepalive); board still enumerated at same MAC = NOT in ROM download mode; forward-task can't wedge on a DTR toggle
(USB-JTAG egress drops-when-unread, never blocks). Did NOT touch the board.
**★ BEARER-OWNER DECISIONS LOCKED (composer eb0bc75 + android, 2026-07-12):** LoRa REAL + WiFi REAL + BLE dark.
**(a) fw inject-per-transport harness CANCELLED** (composer #2 — no no-RF sim leg needed; removed from open items).
**(b) NEW hive task #66 (composer #1), GATED on supervisor GO:** stand a 2nd LoRa node at SF7 (`benchsf7`) as the
R2-PROVISION §3.2 JOIN counterparty to the XIAO (android is phone-provisioner ONLY). Deps on GO: 2nd SX1262 board
attached (RAK DISCONNECTED — need Roy hw) + a JOIN-role build (not keyless xiaobridge). **BLE-REAL FINALIZED (composer 0b2d0bd)** — not skip. Reflash `xiaobridge,ble` still HELD but ADDITIVE (keeps LoRa
bridge + adds ble_task); trigger = AFTER (a) WiFi leg proven AND (b) android BlueZ central built, at a convenient
break in android's live capture. **✅ compile-verified locally (xtensa esp toolchain): `xiaobridge,ble,benchsf7`
builds GREEN (warnings-only) = no feature-unification blocker.** **⚠ compile-green ≠ coex-proven** — BLE+WiFi+LoRa on
the one S3 radio is metal-only at reflash time; full ELF owed at the reflash window (NOT staged now — fw may change).

ORDERING CONTRACT (honoured): write payload(verify-before-write)->finish->write prefix->SWAP MAGIC LAST (single commit anchor; crash-before-magic=no-swap=safe; corrupt-after=boot-gate Err=erase+clear=fail-closed). **(b) prefix placement = MY metal (doesn't affect core's finish()): leaning DEDICATED METADATA REGION over in-DFU-trailer** — SAFETY: embassy-boot swap uses DFU's extra pages (DFU=ACTIVE+2pg) as rotation SCRATCH, so an in-DFU-end trailer is clobbered mid-swap; survivable on a FRESH boot (read before prepare_boot) but a POWER-LOSS-MID-SWAP RESUME would read a corrupt trailer + partially-rotated payload → re-verify fails → clearing magic mid-swap BRICKS a half-swapped ACTIVE. **⚠ SAFETY-CRITICAL GATE RULE (mine, codex-refute): verify ONLY on a FRESH (not-started) swap; NEVER re-verify/cancel an in-progress one — let embassy-boot resume.** A metadata region (never swap-touched) makes the prefix always-readable + sidesteps this. capacity() = full DFU_usable (region) OR DFU_usable-201 (if trailer). **FULL FLOW — RECEIVE(core receiver): reassemble header||sig → OwnedOtaApply::start[early-reject] → feed payload→DFU[0..] → finish → (applied,sink,prefix) → I write prefix+magic. BOOT(my bootloader): magic pending & FRESH? → read prefix(header,sig) → verify_staged_slot(header,sig,DFU[0..payload_len] page-streamed,ctx) → Ok=prepare/swap; Err=erase DFU+clear magic.** Core BUILDING the receiver (return-prefix). Gate wiring next block: re-vendor → wire (incl fresh-vs-resume logic + region placement) → compile → codex-refute.

**★★★ 2026-07-13 — cad8b57 HELD (hive-codex CRITICAL, correctly caught); SUPERSEDE with a redesigned local successor (GO, compile-only, no push/flash until twin-clean).** cad8b57 (bootloader gate) + ec29da4 (re-vendor) = LOCAL commits, UNPUSHED. Parked app edits = stash 6dcfccc (embassy_boot relink @0x24000 + the insufficient 201→204 align). **Confirmed defects (all real vs the exact release ELF):** C1 approval guard DEAD — gate_flag@201, 201%4≠0 → Nvmc Unaligned → optimizer removed the approve write → NO durable approval → power-cut brick (most reproducible fact). C2 reject ignores STATE-erase failure → erased bytes copied into ACTIVE. H4 persona only "sealed" — no BPROT/ACL, app owns unrestricted Nvmc → app compromise rewrites anchor/bootloader. **REFUTED/PROVEN:** 4K STATE OK ((2+4·109)·4=1752B<4096) — KEEP + assert formula; alloc stub not in ELF (r2-trust alloc DCE'd) — keep as drift-backstop + ELF-symbol test.
**CORRECTED MAP (successor):** BOOTLOADER 0x0-0x20000 | STATE 0x20000-0x21000 (4K, proven) | OTA-META 0x21000-0x22000 (candidate prefix+approval) | PERSONA 0x22000-0x24000 | ACTIVE 0x24000-0x91000 (436K/109pg) | DFU 0x91000-0xFF000 (440K/110pg = ACTIVE+1, the documented min) | JOURNAL 0xFF000-0x100000 (4K confirmed-floor, OUTSIDE the swap). **SUCCESSOR REQUIREMENTS (GO):** (1) ONE shared geometry source (app+boot+ota.rs+persona) + build-time overlap/boundary KATs. (2) ALWAYS-VERIFY, gated on embassy-boot's OWN progress counter — NO separate approval record/digest (supervisor Occam+security refutation 2026-07-13, VERIFIED vs embassy-boot-0.7.0 source). Why the digest was dropped: (a) the payload-SHA256 (the expensive part) is paid EITHER WAY (verify checks payload_hash; skip recomputes the digest over the same bytes) — skip saves ONLY the Ed25519 (~tens of ms) ONCE PER OTA (fresh swap), not per boot (normal State::Boot = zero crypto); (b) the digest adds ZERO security — a flash-writing attacker forges the skip in BOTH models (writes record = SHA256(their header‖sig‖payload); bootloader recomputes over their DFU, matches, skips), identical to forging the progress counter; both rely SOLELY on H4 ACL flash-lock. Ground truth (boot_loader.rs): read_state()==Swap for BOTH fresh & in-progress (magic-only); swap() physically ROTATES DFU↔ACTIVE pages, so mid-swap the DFU payload is scrambled/unverifiable; at current_progress()==0 NOTHING is written yet (first op touches only the DFU scratch page at progress→1; first DFU-payload overwrite not until progress≥2) ⇒ progress==0 is a HARD pristine-DFU guarantee. Gate: State::Swap && progress==0 ⇒ FRESH ⇒ read header+sig from OTA-META + stream pristine DFU payload ⇒ full verify_staged_slot (Ed25519 + SHA256==payload_hash + seq>floor) ⇒ PASS → call prepare_boot (starts swap); FAIL → checked-reject. State::Swap && progress>0 ⇒ swap already begun (scrambled) ⇒ NEVER verify, NEVER reject/erase ⇒ pass straight to prepare_boot (embassy resumes). Power-cut in the verify→prepare window leaves progress==0 ⇒ next boot re-verifies pristine DFU (idempotent). The durable "already-authorized" signal is embassy-boot's progress counter itself — no record to write/bind. NOTE: this reads STATE progress words directly (magic@0, valid-marker@WRITE_SIZE, progress@2·WRITE_SIZE+, per embassy-boot 0.7/0.12) — KAT-pin this layout + re-verify on any embassy-boot bump. (3) checked reject — prove STATE non-SWAP (readback) before DFU erase, else fail-stop. (4) payload gate — 0<len≤ACTIVE_LEN, PT_FIRMWARE_FULL, bootable-vector sanity, USE VerifiedUpdate. (5) split dev-bench vs prod DeviceContext (prod = persona/board/device/battery, fail-closed if unavailable). (6) confirmed floor in the SEPARATE atomic JOURNAL page + pending/confirm lifecycle, NO floor=0 fallback. (7) H4 BPROT/ACL — NOT a permitted follow-up for a prod-compilable successor (coordinator correction 2026-07-13): the PROD bootloader build MUST apply reset-time BPROT/ACL protecting BOOTLOADER (0x0-0x20000) + PERSONA (0x22000-0x24000) so a compromised app cannot rewrite the anchor/bootloader, AND partition-wrap the app's Nvmc writes to its own regions; the ONLY unprotected build is an EXPLICITLY-NAMED dev/bench feature; a prod build without protection MUST fail-closed at COMPILE time (compile_error!/const-assert), never silently ship unprotected. Implemented WITH increment 2 (bootloader). ★ ACCEPTANCE (exact re-pass, coordinator 2026-07-13): there must be NO production path that boots with a WRITABLE bootloader/persona — every prod build either boots ACL-protected or does not compile; only the explicit dev/bench feature boots unprotected. (8) falsifiers: power-cut@every write/erase/swap-boundary, stale-approval/new-candidate, map-overlap, reject-fail, floor. LOCAL commit only → exact hive-codex re-pass. DO-NOT-FLASH + Roy tg_pk gate stand.
**★ APP-SEAM FLASHSINK SUB-INCREMENT SPEC (pickup-ready; GATED behind a clean re-review of 9135db2 — do NOT start until re-pass clean; supervisor sequencing).** Files = `rak4630-fw/platforms/rak4630/{src/ota.rs, src/main.rs, build.rs}`. Contract (core-blessed staging ruling + my OTA-META metadata-region choice + F1):
> (1) **ota.rs consume rak-geometry:** `SLOT_B_BASE`→`DFU_ORIGIN` (0x91000), `SLOT_SIZE`/`capacity()`→`ACTIVE_LEN` (0x6D000; matches the boot gate `payload_size≤ACTIVE_LEN` bound). (2) **★F1 app-half — FULL-SLOT ERASE:** `begin()` MUST erase the WHOLE DFU slot `DFU[0..DFU_LEN]` (not just payload-rounded), so the unauthenticated tail `DFU[payload_size..ACTIVE_LEN]` is 0xFF — ELSE the boot gate's tail-all-0xFF assert (9135db2) REJECTS a legit image. (3) **Receiver flow (#19/#35):** use `r2_update::OtaReceiver` (import the SIGNED one BY NAME — NOT the legacy unsigned `r2_hive_core::ota::OtaReceiver`): `new(ctx, PT_FIRMWARE_FULL, FlashSink)` → `push(&[u8])->Result<(RxProgress, consumed), RxError>` (preserve `sdu[consumed..]` post-package bytes) → `finish(self)->(AppliedUpdate, S, prefix:[u8;201])`. `abort()` idempotent + safe after a FAILED/partial `begin()`. (4) **commit_swap (ORDER = the core atomicity contract):** payload→DFU[0..] via FlashSink (verify-before-write) → finish → write `prefix[201]` (header137+sig64) → `OTA_META[0..201]` → set STATE `[0xF0;4]` SWAP_MAGIC **LAST** (plain Nvmc; embassy-boot magic word). Crash anywhere before the magic = no swap = old image boots (safe); corrupt after = boot-gate `verify_staged_slot` Err = fail-closed. (5) persona read `0x12000`→`PERSONA_ORIGIN` (0x22000). (6) app `build.rs` FLASH origin→`ACTIVE_ORIGIN` (0x24000) + VTOR reloc; reconcile parked stash `6dcfccc` (KEEP its embassy_boot relink@0x24000 + VTOR; DROP the obsolete 201→204 align — no approval record anymore). ## 🔨🚧 BUILDING — P3 USB-PAIR simple-secure PERIPHERAL SM (task #67) — supervisor GO 2026-07-12 against R2-PROVISION v0.50 @0f61c81
**★ GO #4 = BUILD ORDER (supervisor 2026-07-12):** build the simple pairing PERIPHERAL SM INTO the xiaobridge fw against twin-clean **v0.50 @`0f61c81`** (verified: ancestor of specs HEAD aff328a on spec-conformance-v0.2), regenerate vectors, re-verify terminal MACs, THEN reflash the XIAO so pairing lights over the live USB link (android runs PairingHost over ttyACM1 = the bench-critical reflash). **✅ SPEC READ @0f61c81 (scratchpad/R2-PROVISION-0f61c81.md §5.3.4 lines 448-798).** Frame vocab (R2-USB §3.7 control `[0xFF]‖CBOR({0:msg_type,1:fields})`): 4 PAIR_HELLO_HOST host→p `{}` · 5 PAIR_COMMIT p→host `{1:commit(32)}` · 13 PAIR_HOST_REVEAL host→p `{1:eph_pk_host(32),2:nonce_host(32)}` · 6 PAIR_REVEAL p→host `{1:eph_pk_p(32),2:nonce_p(32)}` · 7 PAIR_CONFIRM host→p `{1:confirm_mac(16)}` · 8 PAIR_DONE p→host `{1:done_mac(16)}` · 14 PAIR_ACK host→p `{1:ack_mac(16)}` · 9 RECONNECT_CHALLENGE host→p `{1:nonce_rc(16)}` · 10 RECONNECT_RESPONSE p→host `{1:tag(16)}` · 11 PAIR_ABORT either `{1:reason tstr}`. (msg_type 12=observation, 15=retired.) **PERIPHERAL SM:** recv HELLO(4)→RETAIN persisted key, gen fresh eph+nonce, send COMMIT(5); recv HOST_REVEAL(13); send REVEAL(6); Z=X25519, reject all-zero→ABORT{bad_key}; recv CONFIRM(7) verify confirm-host MAC; send DONE(8); recv ACK(14) verify ack-host MAC→**PERSIST K**. Reconnect: recv CHALLENGE(9)→tag=HMAC(link_key,"r2-usb-reconnect-v1"‖nonce_rc‖usb_link_id)[..16]→RESPONSE(10); activation host-local (peripheral proves to host only). Idempotent in-session dup (RAM, 60s terminal timeout): dup CONFIRM→resend DONE, dup ACK→no-op. Key preservation: persisted key retained until final ACK-verify; re-pair on any doubt (no journal/gen/rotation/crash-recovery). transcript = eph_pk_host‖eph_pk_p‖nonce_host‖nonce_p (128B). usb_link_id = CAPS hive_id_bytes (16B) = HKDF("r2-usb-link-v1",device_master_secret,"")[..16].
**✅ TERMINAL MACs RE-VERIFIED byte-exact vs v0.50 (supervisor's re-verify check DONE):** usb_pair.rs labels + asserted hex == spec UP14/UP18 (confirm `4e4c5ff2…`/done `08ba274f…`/ack `1ec03c3d…`/reconnect `2f62edaa…`); KDF domains did NOT move (spec line 570: byte-exact constructions unchanged, naming-only). 14 usb_pair tests green. Crypto restored @5fc3a20 is spec-valid — no revector needed.
**⚠ SCOPE BOUND (spec §5.3.4 lines 456-460, 573-602):** pairing establishes `link_key` ONLY. Key-bearing USB-SAS join (§3 JoinInvite/JoinResponse group-key install) is SPEC-GATED **fail-closed** until the owed `JoinInvite`↔`link_key` invite-MAC binding lands — do NOT implement join key install; the SM ends at link_key + reconnect.

## (was 🔒 HOLD) — P3 USB-PAIR X25519 security finding (android-codex cross-impl, 2026-07-12) — CONFIRMED real in hive; fix CANON-GATED + cross-impl-aligned
android-codex flagged that android P3a AND hive share two P3 (R2-PROVISION §5.3.4 USB pairing) gaps. **BOTH CONFIRMED against hive ground truth:**
1. **No contributory-key rejection (defense-in-depth MUST).** `usb_pair::shared_secret` (usb_pair.rs:68-73) returns `*z.as_bytes()` with NO `z.was_contributory()` check — a zero/low-order `peer_pk` forces Z=0. **⚠ THREAT NARROWED (android-codex + specs advisory 2026-07-12 — my earlier "MITM defeat / attacker-known SAS" framing was TOO STRONG):** the SAS is TRANSCRIPT-BOUND (usb_pair.rs `sas_code` HKDFs Z over eph_pk_host‖eph_pk_periph‖nonce_host‖nonce_periph — verified), so classic MITM key-SUBSTITUTION is ALREADY caught by the human SAS comparison. Contributory-reject is a **defense-in-depth MUST** (specs-confirmed), NOT the sole MITM guard. Still LIVE-REACHABLE (consumed at usb.rs:812 inside the `UsbSession` P3 state machine) + a real gap to close. Negative vector = **UP14** (UP13 is already usb_link_id — specs typo flagged); planned abort reason = dedicated **bad_key** (pending canon).
2. **zeroize hygiene gap.** `x25519-dalek` in Cargo.toml:43 is `default-features=false, features=["static_secrets"]` — NO `zeroize` feature, so StaticSecret/SharedSecret lack ZeroizeOnDrop despite R2-PROVISION's destroy-eph_sk/Z MUST. **⚠ NUANCE: enabling the feature alone is INSUFFICIENT** — `shared_secret` returns a plain `[u8;32]` copy and usb.rs stores Z/link_key/eph_sk as plain arrays (never zeroized); proper destruction needs `Zeroizing<[u8;32]>` on the STORED secrets in usb.rs, done together with the feature.
**DECISION = HOLD, do NOT patch unilaterally (spec-first + cross-impl parity).** The rejection semantics need canon — specs/android escalation ACTIVE to pin was_contributory-rejection in R2-PROVISION §5.3.4 + a negative KAT. Patching hive's `shared_secret` API (→Result/Option) now would DIVERGE from Android's approach + pre-empt the canon. **When canon lands: (a) reject `!was_contributory()` at the primitive with the dedicated `bad_key` abort, aligned with Android, (b) add UP14 (low-order peer_pk → bad_key reject), (c) `Zeroizing<>` the stored Z/link_key/eph_sk + enable the x25519-dalek zeroize feature — ALL in one coordinated pass, both impls together.** ⚠ **The actual adaptive-SAS-grind blocker is SEPARATE (android-codex leading): first-pair `HELLO_HOST` exposes the host contribution BEFORE the peripheral COMMIT — HOLD the P3 state-machine CHOREOGRAPHY until that ordering + the canon land.** **✅ Android's PRIMITIVE is already hardened (a03d949); so the remaining cross-impl coordination = state-machine choreography + Zeroizing + the exact abort bytes, AFTER the ordering fix + canon land (per android-codex 2026-07-12).** Reject prevents unsafe Z=0 reuse; a malicious endpoint only ever knows its OWN session (NOT the honest endpoints' keys) — do NOT overframe as classic-MITM key-recovery. Confirmed both gaps to android-codex; holding P3 hardening. Folds around the P2 v2-conformance work (same usb.rs surface).
**➕ msg7/8 KEY-CONFIRMATION / DESYNC finding (hive-codex, specs ruling design-only 2026-07-12 — v0.34 NOT LANDED) — CONFIRMED against ground truth, HELD:** (a) `handle_pair_done` (usb.rs:843-859) ignores the DONE body (`_body`) + persists `link_keys.store(&lk)` with NO MAC check; (b) `user_confirms` (usb.rs:898) emits an EMPTY PAIR_CONFIRM (no MAC); (c) `pending_link_key` derived BEFORE the operator prompt (usb.rs:832, eager). **Threat = availability/key-confirmation desync (an active USB attacker blocks CONFIRM + injects DONE → host-only persistence, or injects CONFIRM at peripheral → inverse desync), NOT key recovery.** **SPECS-DRAFTED FIX (design only, apply in the coordinated pass when v0.34 lands):** PAIR_CONFIRM(7)=`HMAC-SHA256(link_key, 'r2-usb-pair-confirm-host-v1' ‖ transcript)`; PAIR_DONE(8)=`HMAC-SHA256(link_key, 'r2-usb-pair-confirm-peripheral-v1' ‖ transcript)`; `transcript = eph_pk_host‖eph_pk_peripheral‖nonce_host‖nonce_peripheral`; verify CONSTANT-TIME; fail→`bad_key`+destroy pending; **each side persists ONLY after a valid peer MAC.** Eager pending key = conformant IFF destroyed-on-decline (specs; canon wording changes derive→persist/retain) — current wipe (usb.rs:274-281) is BEST-EFFORT only (real zeroize owed = same Zeroizing pass). **Also CONFIRMED-current + CONTESTED-canon: msg4 sends host contribution before commit (usb.rs:723-745, commit:None) — specs working tree has an uncommitted alternate empty-msg4/msg13; choreography still contested → HOLD.** **Also: `run_session` lacks an ENFORCED 60s deadline (documented at usb.rs:126/904 but no Instant/Duration timer) — retain for the coordinated rewrite.** hive-codex asked specs to rule; I do NOT patch locally (specs v0.34 mid-edit/uncommitted; Android confirms no persist path today + is holding its terminal path). **ONE coordinated P3 rewrite when v0.34 lands: was_contributory-reject + MAC'd CONFIRM/DONE + persist-after-peer-MAC + destroy-on-decline Zeroizing + enforced 60s deadline + UP14 negative KAT — all cross-impl-aligned with Android byte-for-byte.**

## 📻 RADAR (core, no action — pending specs): R2-UPDATE v0.54 §2.4 abi_hash-nonzero-for-CODE
A CODE-bearing OTA payload MUST carry nonzero abi_hash. RAK monolithic firmware OTA = firmware_full (0x01) with abi_hash=0 + host_abi_hash=[0;8]. Rule AMBIGUOUS: reading X (strict) → starts rejecting; reading Y (exempts full-base-replacement, which a monolithic MCU image arguably IS) → gate only plugin_module 0x07 (doesn't exist yet) → **zero RAK impact**. Core LEANS Y, flagged specs, HOLDING the core gate — nothing changes for RAK OTA now. IF specs rules X: set RAK firmware abi_hash to a real host-ABI value + host_abi_hash to match. Core confirms on ruling.
- **CRITICAL #1 — anti-rollback FAIL-OPEN (ota_tcp.rs):** load_anti_rollback() returns (0,0) on an NVS OPEN/READ ERROR (not just absent) → a corrupt/unavailable NVS floors anti-rollback to 0 → an OLD signed seq is ADMITTED (downgrade); and commit/stage/clear discard every NVS write error (let _ = set_u32) → a failed floor advance is SILENT. FIX (agreed, fail-CLOSED): NVS ops return Result + refuse-to-START an OTA if the floor is unreadable + durably stage {seq,payload_hash} BEFORE esp_ota set_boot + reconcile pending after mark-valid (same discipline as the RAK FlashSink).
- **✅ CRITICAL #1 (dup early ota_health_check) LANDED @core 42ff54a** — removed the early confirmer that marked the OTA partition VALID on weak checks (FNV/CBOR + random-key RBID) BEFORE WiFi/identity/trust (cancelled auto-rollback pre-real-health + left non-PENDING so confirm_or_rollback cleared pending_seq without advancing current_seq = stale replayable floor). Now confirm_or_rollback_on_boot() (after real §5 health) is the SOLE confirm owner + only esp_ota_mark_app_valid callsite. Blind-authored (core verified by reasoning); **I compile + metal-verify on espup.**
- **✅ BOTH CRITICALS LANDED — combined platforms/esp32 state BUILDABLE (core, 2026-07-11):** #1 @42ff54a + #2 @56945dd. ★ #2 ALSO fixed a compile-unblock: the esp32 signed-OTA DeviceContext was MISSING host_abi_hash + core_abi_version (drifted since M2 v0.50) → the OTA path (ota_tcp handle_start_signed) didn't compile vs workspace r2-update; #2 adds them ([0;8]/0, esp32 runs no dynamic modules). #2 = 6 NVS fns→Result (ABSENT=Ok(0) vs FAULT=Err); load_anti_rollback Err→REFUSE OTA (never gate vs a faulted floor); stage_pending_seq DURABLY before esp_ota set_boot; confirm fail-SAFE toward not-bricking. ## 🧩 WASM HOST — LINKABLE BASE (NEW workstream, Roy GO 2026-07-10, task #64; parallel to RAK)
Roy ruled BUILD the linkable base; hive owns the **wasm HOST** (base HOSTS wasm ensemble modules = Level 2, greenfield — NOT r2-hive-wasm, which is R2 compiled TO wasm). Ref: r2-specifications docs/proposals/R2-LINKABLE-BASE-AND-VARIANT-MANAGEMENT-2026-07-10.md (D.3 steps 4-5). **Prep design committed: docs/WASM-HOST-LINKABLE-BASE-PREP.md (c709e23).**
- **Two ABI surfaces** (both = the §12.4 Plugin trait lowered to repr(C) per proposal A.5.3): module-EXPORTS (execute/init/poll → wasm ptr+len) + host-IMPORTS (the capabilities.requires §12.3 syscall surface = "the host-import surface"). A wasm module becomes a Rust Plugin impl trampolining into its exports → plugs into existing engine dispatch.
- **Phasing (D.3 4-5, core A.5 binding):** std host (wasmtime) + browser (native WebAssembly) FIRST; then esp32s3+PSRAM wasm3; **nrf52840 = ONE bounded (<=32KB) boot-reserved wasm3 slot only** (A.5.1 — general multi-module REFUTED; binding constraint = 64KB-page CONTIGUITY on MMU-less heap, not total RAM). **Level-0 hot-path/crypto NEVER modularized** (A.5.4 — route/dedup/wire/CBOR/FNV, radio io_task, HMAC/HKDF/Ed25519). Host = orchestration-class only.
- **✅ M1 LANDED — gate LIFTED.** R2-PLUGIN v0.6 §12.4.3 Frozen ABI RATIFIED (specs 73af517, in my local checkout; read fully). Froze: AbiResponse[128]/AbiError[64]/AbiResult (repr(C,u8)); PluginVTableV1 (repr(C), abi_version FIRST, id, execute/init/poll/name extern C, inst=*mut c_void); ONE export `__r2_plugin_vtable_v1`; init/poll required (r2-forge no-op); abi_hash = SHA-256 over canonical schema, load gate order = verify sig → abi_hash EXACT-match → instantiate. 4 rulings: 8B abi_hash trunc in UpdateHeader / exact-match v1 / one-vtable-per-module / init-poll-required-noop. core implements the repr(C) types + r2-forge shim-gen + vtable KAT.
- **✅ WASM-PROJECTION CO-DESIGN — CANDIDATE DRAFTED (d2d8302), handed to specs for ratification as §12.4.3.1.** §12.4.3 froze the NATIVE repr(C) vtable; the L2 boundary needs a byte-for-byte WASM PROJECTION (host + r2-forge module must agree). Per core's spec-first ask it lands NORMATIVE (specs-ratified §12.4.3.1), not a bilateral handshake. Draft: `docs/WASM-PROJECTION-12.4.3.1-CANDIDATE.md`. **core's f866c3f adversarial review ACCEPTED IN FULL** (2 corrections):
  - **8 module exports** (CONFIRMED sound by core): memory / global __r2_abi_version / func __r2_abi_hash(out_ptr writes FULL 32B) / global __r2_plugin_id / r2_init(result_ptr) / r2_execute(cmd,dptr,dlen,result_ptr) / r2_poll(ev_out,buf,cap)->i32 / r2_name(buf,cap)->i32. inst DROPPED (one module=one plugin, Ruling 3).
  - **CORRECTION accepted — AbiResult = BYTE-EXACT native repr(C,u8) 136B IMAGE** (NOT my earlier 132B len-prefixed guess): tag@0, payload@4 (AbiError u32 forces union-align 4), field order data[128]-then-len u16 (Ok) / code u32,desc[64],desc_len (Err). ⇒ core's EXISTING native AbiResult KAT pins the wasm buffer too — ONE layout, zero separate encoding. Host supplies >=136B result_ptr.
  - **full 32B abi_hash v1 = c37f504d4c2a9d8c1f5bc214aa229b4ae8c0d88897a49cce519814d8915a817e** (core provided; first 8B = c37f504d4c2a9d8c). TWO forms (targeting≠authz, B.2.0): FULL 32B = load-gate exact-match (module exports, host embeds, Ruling 2); 8B trunc = UpdateHeader/recipe compat, header-sig-authenticated (Ruling 1). Monolithic images = all-zero.
  - load-gate order confirmed: verify sig → abi_hash 32B EXACT → instantiate+read exports.
- **✅ specs ENDORSED the §12.4.3.1 design IN FULL + ruled it UNGATED** (version bump only, no vector co-bump; core supplies the wasm-image KAT). Endorsed: native-image-136B AbiResult (the right Occam call — one canonical layout, two projections), the two abi_hash forms, inst-drop (Ruling 3). specs could NOT read my cross-repo candidate doc from its worktree → **I handed specs the FULL §12.4.3.1 text INLINE** (fleet, plain-text no-backticks). **specs is write-blocked this turn** (read-only sandbox mirror) → will LAND R2-PLUGIN §12.4.3.1 (from my inline text) + R2-UPDATE v0.47 when write access returns.

  hive — canonically a DEV device) sees ALL neighbours as Prod → equality fails → try_directed skips all +
  flood finds zero → Drop(NoViableNeighbour) on everything → every dev mesh dies on uptake. Only all-prod
  meshes survive. Core's don't-downgrade offer is necessary but insufficient (never-declared entries read
  Prod forever).
- COUNTER-PROPOSAL (to core; canon nuance to specs): Observation.build_mode → Option<BuildMode>; None = this
  observation carries no declaration; entry keeps sticky last-DECLARED mode; never-declared entries are
  MODE-TRANSPARENT in §4.4 viability. Key distinction argued: absence-of-the-BYTE in an observed beacon =
  declared prod (ruled, retroactive, stands); absence of ANY beacon observation is NOT a declaration.
  §3A safety unaffected (refusal arms sit where declarations exist by construction); honest residual flagged
  (a never-beacon-ingesting prod engine can't demote a dev neighbour via §4.4 alone — admission still
  excludes).

## 🧭 R2-BUILDMODE §4.4 VIABILITY API IN FLIGHT (2026-07-06 — core proposed, I ack'd with ONE counter)
- Core proposed the r2-route mode-viability shape (the gate on my §3A drop arms): BuildMode on Observation +
  NeighbourEntry (resolved at MY decoder, absence-is-prod there — r2-route never guesses), own-mode on the engine,
  equality added to the is_viable gate in try_directed + build_flood_plan (selection-not-formation, §2.1.3 stands),
  getters (NeighbourEntry::build_mode / RouteEngine::my_build_mode) so the dataplane frame-DROP arms stay my half.
- ACKED the shape; COUNTERED the two-variant enum: unknown wire values (the deliberately-skipped 0x01, a future
  0x03) must NOT collapse to Prod — that would make an undefined class silently viable inside prod meshes. Asked
  for raw u8 OR BuildMode{Prod,Dev,Other(u8)} (my preference); plain equality is then fail-closed AND
  forward-compatible for free (class-N nodes route among themselves, non-viable to both shipped modes).
- (b) answered: CTOR ARG and NO setter at all (v0.4 persona catch — mode flip = reflash + RE-PROVISION; a runtime
  set_my_build_mode is a mutation surface canon forbids). (c): closed set today (the legacy-BLE gap was the
  missing codec FIELD, ruled v0.26/v0.27, not a third mode) but size for extension via Other(u8).
- My decode mapping committed in the ack: LoRa len15/16→Prod; len17 p[16]=0x02→Dev, 0x00→Prod (belt-and-braces,
  my emitter never sends 17B-prod), else Other; BLE AD-offset-22 byte gets the same mapping.
- ✅ RULED SAME-DAY (R2-BUILDMODE v0.6, specs HEAD): unknown-not-Prod blessed AS PROPOSED. Mode homogeneity =
  EQUALITY on the declared class value; unknown values (reserved 0x01, future 0x03) are cross-class to BOTH
  shipped modes — non-viable + refused at connection/admission exactly like dev-vs-prod; same-value peers
  mutually viable; unknown-collapse-to-prod explicitly FORBIDDEN as fail-open. Other(u8)+plain-equality = the
  canon-named realization. FUTURE-PROOFING PIN: if a reserved value is ever ACTIVATED (0x01 prod-bench etc.),
  its interop relation gets ruled explicitly AT ACTIVATION — equality is only the meanwhile default, nothing
  pre-judged. Also folded: the §4 wasm-bridge registry row now names r2-hive-wasm's wasm-bindgen surface as THE
  observability seam (Roy-confirmed 3-way wording). Core relayed — nothing waits on specs; API can land.
- When core lands the r2-route side: wire the Observation feed + §3A drop arms same day (task #50c).
- ✅ BLE HALF CLOSED SAME-DAY (core codec b420fb3 → my emit fw 37f23b1 → vector to specs, one cycle):
  re-vendored r2-discovery wholesale from b420fb3; build_class = BUILD_CLASS set at the LegacyBeacon
  construction; SIX local-xtensa arms green (incl. bare field — see below — and the canonical
  field,carrier,loraroute compose) + field×dev gate still fires. Conformance vector generated via the REAL
  codec (scratchpad host crate, asserts: AD-22 placement, round-trips, dev/prod differ in exactly one byte,
  18B truncation decodes prod) and delivered to specs with all inputs stated (demo hk 0xA5×32, hive 0x480E900E,
  epoch 0, sensor class 0x43895E89). LATENT-BREAK FIX en route (got.3 class, PRE-EXISTING — proven red at
  715064a): mesh_broadcast was cfg(ble) but the fr4 SCF-FWD call is carrier-agnostic → bare field never
  compiled AND pure-LoRa field composes had no SCF forward; gate now any(ble,loraroute) + ble-gated ESP-NOW

## 🎯 DARK-BOARD MECHANISM CONVERGED (2026-07-05): stale NVS @0x14000 TG-override, NOT personas — I own the fix procedure (task #42) + DEPROVISION proposal (task #43, HELD)
- **Ground truth (supervisor-codex recorded, refutation accepted):** personas @0x12000 are ALL weave-correct; my earlier key-epoch-on-persona
  framing was wrong at the *storage layer* — the wrong-epoch key lives in the **runtime-PROVISION record @0x14000** (magic R2TG,
  `[magic u32 BE][tg_id u32 BE][key 32B]` = 40 B, own 4 KB sector; `main.rs:2191`), which **OVERRIDES the persona at boot**
  (`main.rs:265-276`, serial line `PROVISIONED TG restored from NVS`). Dark boards D2 (xx:xx:xx / <D2-NVS-TG>) + D4 (xx:xx:xx / <D4-NVS-TG>)
  carry a stale override with tg_id <WEAVE-TG-A> + an OLD-epoch hk → HMAC verify fails → correct fail-closed refusal. Fix = ONE-SECTOR
  clear/overwrite, **NOT** persona rewrite, **NOT** a reflash.
- **The two operational fixes (Roy chooses intent — NO NVS clearing until then; standing directive):**
  - **(A) Roy download-mode erase (human-only, pristine end-state):** `esptool.py --port /dev/ttyACM<n> erase_region 0x14000 0x1000`
    (or `espflash erase-region 0x14000 0x1000`). Erased flash = 0xFF → magic check fails → `read_provisioned_tg()` = None → boot
    falls back to the (weave-correct) persona. ⚠ offset-typo hazard: 0x12000 would kill the persona — the command above is exact.
  - **(B) composer console overwrite (no download mode, NO reboot):** send to each board's OWN tty (steady DTR=1/RTS=0 discipline):
    `PROVISION <D2-NVS-TG> <WEAVE-TG-B> <weave_hk_64hex>` (D2/ACM5) and `PROVISION <D4-NVS-TG> <WEAVE-TG-B> <weave_hk_64hex>` (D4/ACM4).
    <WEAVE-TG-B> = decimal of 0x<WEAVE-TG-A> (the §6 tg_id IS the wire target_group). Path: `parse_provision` validates (exact-32B key) →
    `write_provisioned_tg` erase+write+read-back-verify → ACK `PROVISION-APPLIED wire=… tg_id=…` → io_task swaps GroupHmac +
    target_group LIVE (`main.rs:1074-1085`). Re-runnable/idempotent; failure ACKs PROVISION-ERR, installs nothing.
  - **Trade-off:** (B) leaves override-ACTIVE state (0x14000 keeps shadowing the persona — future hk rotations need another
    PROVISION or an erase); (A) restores persona-governed state but needs the human cable dance. Same end TG either way.
- **Blast radius (either option): ZERO collateral.** Flash map, each its own 4 KB sector: persona@0x12000 · board-profile@0x13000 ·
  **TG-override@0x14000 (the only target)** · MASK@0x15000 · SENDTO@0x16000 · RPF1 role@0x17000 · anti-rollback@0x18000 ·
  LBL1 label@0x1B000 · ota_0@0x20000. **NO apiary-role detachment** — role lives @0x17000 + is derivable, fully independent of the
  TG override; hive_id unchanged (persona master_secret). Option A's download-mode entry reboots the board (beats reset — fine,
  these are the dark boards, not the #49 beat-discriminator board).
- **Verify after (safe steady-DTR read):** (A) boot shows NO `PROVISIONED TG restored from NVS` line; (B) `PROVISION-APPLIED` +
  `PROVISION installed live` ACKs, no reboot. Then both: HEALTH decodes tg_hash=<WEAVE-TG-A>, nbrs stops the 0↔1 flap, **dlv increments
  on demo traffic** (the decisive falsifier that the hk now verifies).
- **Conditional branch closed:** the "if target_group already <WEAVE-TG-A> AND frames verify → real deliver/LED bug" fork is MOOT under
  the converged mechanism (frames do NOT verify under the stale key) — reopens only if composer's native-frame check refutes.
- **Task #43 (NEW, HELD):** DEPROVISION console verb proposal (clear @0x14000 over console, live-revert to persona hk symmetric with
  the install path). Spec-first via CROSS-HOST-2TG §6 extension; NO firmware change unless Roy explicitly asks.
